  262. 138. Mathbox for Kunhao Zheng
    1. 138.1. Weighted AM-GM inequality

MetaMath theorems

Projective geometries based on Hilbert lattices

@( =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-= Additional set theory definitions =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-= @)

@c fcard @. @c idsumf @. @c idsum @.

@( Extend class notation with finite cardinality (member of NN0 ). @) cfc @a class fcard @.

@( Extend class notation with finite idempotent sum. @) cidsumf @a class idsumf @.

@( Extend class notation with idempotent sum. @) cidsum @a class idsum @.

@{ @d f n p s t u x y @. @( Define finite cardinality. @) df-fcard @a |- fcard = ( x e. _V |-> if ( x e. Fin , ( iota n ( n e. NN /\ E. f f : x -1-1-onto-> ( 1 ... n ) ) ) , ( Undef ` NN0 ) ) ) @.

@( Define finite idempotent sum. @)
df-idsumf @a |- idsumf = ( p e. _V , s e. _V |->
( iota t A. f ( f : ( 1 ... ( fcard ` s ) ) -1-1-onto-> s
     -> t = ( ( p ser f ) ` ( fcard ` s ) ) ) ) ) @.
df-idsumf @a |- idsumf = ( p e. _V , s e. _V |->
( iota t A. f ( f : ( 1 ... ( fcard ` s ) ) -1-1-onto-> s
     -> t = ( ( p ser f ) ` ( fcard ` s ) ) ) ) ) @.

( ( P seq1 F ) ` N )

@( Define idempotent sum. @)
df-idsum @a |- idsum = ( p e. _V , s e. _V |->
    U. { u | E. t ( u = ( p idsumf t ) /\ t C_ s /\ t e. Fin ) } ) @.

@} U. { a | E. t C_ s E. n e. NN0 E. f ( f : ( 1 ... n ) -1-1-onto-> t /\ a = ( ( p seq f ) n ) ) } ) $. df-idsum @a |- idsum = ( p e. _V , f e. _V |-> U. { a | E. t E. g ( t e. Fin /\ t C_ f ) /\ ( g : ( 1 ... ( # t ) ) -1-1-onto-> dom t /\ A. x e. dom g A. y e. dom g ( x < y -> ( g x ) < ( g y ) ) /\ a = ( ( p seq1 ( f o. g ) ) ( # t ) ) ) ) }

@( =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-= Posets and lattices; Hilbert lattices =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-= @)

@( =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-= From groups to Hilbert spaces =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-= @)

@c -vNEW @. @c RVecNEW @. @c SubSpNEW @. @c spanNEW @. @c o+ @. @c Ev @. @c /v @. @c normv @.

@( Extend class notation with vector subtraction. @) cminusv @a class -vNEW @.

@( Extend class notation with class of all right vector spaces. @) crvec @a class RVecNEW @.

@( Extend class notation with set of all subspaces in a vector space. @) cssp @a class SubSpNEW @.

@( Extend class notation with span of a set of vectors. @) cspan @a class spanNEW @.

@( Extend class notation with direct sum. @) coplus @a class o+ @.

@( Extend class notation with vector equivalence classes. @) cev @a class Ev @.

@( Extend class notation with quotient space. @) cqv @a class /v @.

@( Extend class notation with norm of a vector. @) cnormv @a class normv @.

@{ @d a b c e f g h i k m p q r s t u v w x y z @. @( Define vector subtraction. @) df-minusv @a |- -vNEW = ( v e. _V |-> ( x e. ( Base v ) , y e. ( Base v ) |-> ( x ( +g v ) ( ( invg { <. 1 , ( Base v ) >. , <. 2 , ( +g v ) >. } ) ` y ) ) ) ) @.

@( Define class of all right vector spaces. @)
df-rvec @a |- RVecNEW = Struct ( 6 , f , ( f e. DivRingOLD  /\
  E. k E. p E. t E. v E. a E. s (
     ( k = ( Base ` f ) /\ p = ( +g ` f ) /\ t = ( .r ` f ) )
  /\ ( v = ( vbase ` f ) /\ a = ( vadd ` f ) /\ s = ( .s ` f ) )
      /\ ( { <. 1 , v >. , <. 2 , a >. } e. AbelOLD
         /\ A. q e. k A. r e. k A. x e. v A. w e. v
           ( ( ( w s r ) e. v
             /\ ( ( w a x ) s r ) = ( ( w s r ) a ( x s r ) )
             /\ ( w s ( q p r ) ) = ( ( w s q ) a ( w s r ) )
           ) /\ ( ( ( w s q ) s r ) = ( w s ( q t r ) )
             /\ ( w s ( 1r ` f ) ) = w ) ) ) ) ) ) @.

@( Define set of all subspaces of left vector space ` v ` . @)
df-sbsp @a |- SubSpNEW = ( v e. _V |-> { s e. ~P ( vbase ` v )
 | ( ( 0v ` v ) e. s /\ A. x e. s A. y e. s ( x ( vadd ` v ) y ) e. s
    /\ A. x e. ( Base ` v ) A. y e. s ( x ( .s ` v ) y ) e. s ) } ) @.

@( Define span of a set of vectors. @)
df-vspan @a |- spanNEW = ( v e. _V |-> ( m e. ~P ( vbase ` v ) |->
   |^| { s e. ( SubSpNEW ` v ) | m C_ s } ) ) @.

@( Define direct sum of two left vector spaces. @)
df-oplus @a |- o+ = ( v e. _V , w e. _V |-> ( { <. 1 , ( Base ` v ) >. ,
   <. 2 , ( +g ` v ) >. , <. 3 , ( .r ` v ) >. } u. {
   <. 4 , ( ( vbase ` v ) X. ( vbase ` w ) ) >. ,
   <. 5 , ( x e. ( ( vbase ` v ) X. ( vbase ` w ) ) ,
            y e. ( ( vbase ` v ) X. ( vbase ` w ) ) |->
              <. ( ( 1st ` x ) ( vadd ` v ) ( 1st ` y ) ) ,
                 ( ( 2nd ` x ) ( vadd ` w ) ( 2nd ` y ) ) >. ) >. ,
   <. 6 , ( k e. ( Base ` v ) ,
            x e. ( ( vbase ` v ) X. ( vbase ` w ) ) |->
              <. ( k ( .s ` v ) ( 1st ` x ) ) ,
                 ( k ( .s ` w ) ( 2nd ` x ) ) >. ) >. } ) ) @.

@( Define vector equivalence mod ` m ` . @)
df-ev @a |- Ev = ( v e. _V , m e. _V |-> { <. x , y >. |
   ( x e. ( vbase ` v ) /\ y e. ( vbase ` v ) /\
   ( x ( -vNEW ` v ) y ) e. ( vbase ` m ) ) } ) @.

@( Define quotient space. @)
df-quov @a |- /v = ( v e. _V , m e. _V |-> ( { <. 1 , ( Base ` v ) >. ,
   <. 2 , ( +g ` v ) >. , <. 3 , ( .r ` v ) >. } u. {
   <. 4 , ( ( vbase ` v ) /. ( v Ev m ) ) >. ,
   <. 5 , { <. <. a , b >. , c >. | E. x e. ( vbase ` v )
      E. y e. ( vbase ` v ) ( a = [ x ] ( v Ev m )
        /\ b = [ y ] ( v Ev m )
        /\ c = [ ( x ( vadd ` v ) y ) ] ( v Ev m ) ) } >. ,
   <. 6 , { <. <. a , b >. , c >. | ( a e. ( Base ` v ) /\
      E. y e. ( vbase ` v ) ( b = [ y ] ( v Ev m )
        /\ c = [ ( x ( .s ` v ) y ) ] ( v Ev m ) ) ) } >. } ) ) @.

@( Define norm of a vector. @)
df-normv @a |- normv = ( h e. _V |-> ( v ( .i ` h ) v ) ) @.

@}

@( =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-= Hilbert space reconstruction =-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-= @)

@c sumP @. @c Indep @. @c BasesP @. @c rankP @. @c PHyp @. @c ww @. @c WAtoms @. @c PAut @. @c Dil @. @c Trn @. @c trP @. @c DVecA @. @c GrpEndo @. @c DVecAEndo @. @c ERing @. @c TPEndo @. @c DRing @. @c DVecA @. @c DVIsoPre @. @c DVecB @. @c DVecH @. @c ee @. @c DVIsoA @. @c qtr @. @c DVIsoB @. @c DVIsoC @. @c DVIsoH @. @c S_|_ @. @c Ropp @. @c Vldual @. @c vecdom @. @c ker @. @c mapd @. @c eimage @. @c hmap @. @c gmap @. @c HLtoHil @.

@( Extend class notation with projective subspace sum. @) csump @a class sumP @.

@( Extend class notation with set of all sets of independent points. @) cindep @a class Indep @.

@( Extend class notation with all bases for projective subspaces. @) cbasesp @a class BasesP @.

@( Extend class notation with rank of projective subspace @m@. @) crankp @a class rankP @.

@( Extend class notation with set of all (projective) hyperplanes. @) cphyp @a class PHyp @.

@( Extend class notation with fiducial hyperplane. @) cww @a class ww @.

@( Extend class notation with W points. @) cwpointsN @a class WAtoms @.

@( Extend class notation with set of all projective automorphisms. @) cpautN @a class PAut @.

@( Extend class notation with set of all dilations. @) cdilN @a class Dil @.

@( Extend class notation with set of all translations. @) ctrnN @a class Trn @.

@( Extend class notation with trace of a translation @f@. @) ctrp @a class trP @.

@( Extend class notation with translation group. @) ctgrp @a class TGrp @.

@( Extend class notation with group endomorphisms of @G@. @) cgrpendo @a class GrpEndo @.

@( Extend class notation with translation group endomorphisms. @) ctgrpendo @a class TGrpEndo @.

@( Extend class notation with endomorphism ring. @) cering @a class ERing @.

@( Extend class notation with trace-preserving endomorphisms. @) ctpendo @a class TPEndo @.

@( Extend class notation with @\Delta@-ring. @) cdring @a class DRing @.

@( Extend class notation with constructed vector space A. @) cdveca @a class DVecA @.

@( Extend class notation with preliminary projective subspace isomorphism. @) cdvisopre @a class DVIsoPre @.

@( Extend class notation with constructed vector space B. @) cdvecb @a class DVecB @.

@( Extend class notation with constructed vector space. @) cdvech @a class DVecH @.

@( Extend class notation with e vector. @) cee @a class ee @.

@( Extend class notation with projective subspace isomorphism A. @) cdvisoa @a class DVIsoA @.

@( Extend class notation with q-translation. @) cqtr @a class qtr @.

@( Extend class notation with projective subspace isomorphism B. @) cdvisob @a class DVIsoB @.

@( Extend class notation with projective subspace isomorphism C. @) cdvisoc @a class DVIsoC @.

@( Extend class notation with projective subspace isomorphism. @) cdvisoh @a class DVIsoH @.

@( Extend class notation with constructed orthocomplement. @) csoc @a class S_|_ @.

@( Extend class notation with opposite ring. @) cropp @a class Ropp @.

@( Extend class notation with left dualvector space. @) cvldual @a class Vldual @.

@( Extend class notation with vector domain. @) cvecdom @a class vecdom @.

@( Extend class notation with kernel of a functional. @) cker @a class ker @.

@( Extend class notation with one-dimensional subspace map. @) cmapd @a class mapd @.

@( Extend class notation with e vector image. @) ceimage @a class eimage @.

@( Extend class notation with h map. @) chmap @a class hmap @.

@( Extend class notation with g map. @) cgmap @a class gmap @.

@( Extend class notation with Hilbert space constructed from Hilbert lattice. @) chltohil @a class HLtoHil @.

@{ @d a b d e f g h k l m n p q r s t u v w x y z @. @( Define projective sum of a set of subspaces. @) df-sump @a |- sumP = ( l e. _V |-> ( s e. ~P ( PSubSp l ) |-> ( ( +P l ) idsumf s ) ) ) @.

@( Define set of all sets of independent points. @)
df-indep @a |- Indep = ( l e. _V |-> { s e. ~P ( Points ` l )
| A. a A. b ( ( ( a u. b ) = s /\ ( a i^i b ) = (/) ) ->
  ( ( ( sumP ` l ) ` a ) i^i ( ( sumP ` l ) ` b ) ) = (/) ) } ) @.

@( Define all bases for projective subspace @m@. @)
df-basesp @a |- BasesP = ( l e. _V , m e. _V |-> { s e. ( Indep ` l )
  | ( ( sumP ` l ) ` s ) = m } ) @.

@( Define rank of projective subspace @m@. @)
df-rankp @a |- rankP = ( l e. _V , m e. _V |-> ( iota r
A. b e. ( l TopBases m ) r = ( card ` b ) ) ) @.

@( Define set of all (projective) hyperplanes. @)
df-phyp @a |- PHyp = ( l e. _V |-> { h | E. p e. ( Points ` l )
    h = ( ( _|_P ` l ) ` p ) } ) @.

@( Define fiducial hyperplane. @)
df-ww @a |- ww = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> ( ( _|_P ` l ) ` { p } ) ) @.

@( Define W points. @)
df-wpoints @a |- WAtoms = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> { x e. ( Points ` l )
  | -. x C_ ( l ww p ) } ) @.

@( Define set of all projective automorphisms. @)
df-pautN @a |- PAut = ( l e. _V |-> { f | ( f : ( PSubSp ` l ) -1-1-onto->
  ( PSubSp ` l ) /\ A. x e. ( PSubSp ` l ) A. y e. ( PSubSp ` l )
    ( x C_ y <-> ( f ` x ) C_ ( f ` y ) ) ) } ) @.

@( Define set of all dilations. @)
df-dilN @a |- Dil = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> { f e. ( PAut ` l )
 | A. x e. ( PSubSp ` l ) ( x C_ ( l ww p ) -> ( f ` x ) = x ) } ) @.

@( Define set of all translations. @)
df-trnN @a |- Trn = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> { f e. ( l Dil p )
 | A. q e. ( l WAtoms p ) A. r e. ( l WAtoms p )
    ( ( q ( +P ` l ) ( f ` q ) ) i^i ( l ww p ) )
  = ( ( r ( +P ` l ) ( f ` r ) ) i^i ( l ww p ) ) } ) @.

@( Define trace of a translation ` f ` . @)
df-trp @a |- trP = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> ( f e. ( l Trn p ) |->
 ( iota x ( x e. ( PSubSp ` l ) /\ A. q e. ( l WAtoms p )
    x = ( ( q ( +P ` l ) ( f ` q ) ) i^i ( l ww p ) ) ) ) ) ) @.

@( Define translation group. @)
df-tgrp @a |- TGrp = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> { <. 1 , ( l Trn p ) >. ,
   <. 2 , ( f e. ( l Trn p ) , g e. ( l Trn p ) |-> ( f o. g ) ) >. } ) @.

@( Define group endomorphisms of @G@. @)
df-grpendo @a |- GrpEndo = ( g e. _V |-> { f |

( f : ( Base g ) --> ( Base g ) /\ A. x e. ( Base g ) A. y e. ( Base g ) ( x ( +g g ) y ) = ( ( f x ) ( +g g ) ( f y ) ) ) } ) @.

@( Define translation group endomorphisms. @)
df-tgrpendo @a |- TGrpEndo = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
  ( GrpEndo ` ( l TGrp p ) ) ) @.

@( Define endomorphism ring. @)
df-ering @a |- ERing = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> { <. 1 , ( l TGrpEndo p ) >.
    ,
   <. 2 , ( s e. ( l TGrpEndo p ) , t e. ( l TGrpEndo p ) |->
       ( f e. ( l Trn p ) |-> ( ( s ` f ) o. ( t ` f ) ) ) ) >. ,
   <. 3 , ( s e. ( l TGrpEndo p ) , t e. ( l TGrpEndo p ) |->
       ( f e. ( l Trn p ) |-> ( t ` ( s ` f ) ) ) ) >. } ) @.

@( Define trace-preserving endomorphisms. @)
df-tpendo @a |- TPEndo = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> { s e. ( l TGrpEndo p ) |
 A. f e. ( Base ` ( l TGrp p ) )
     ( ( l trP p ) ` ( s ` f ) ) C_ ( ( l trP p ) ` f ) } ) @.

@( Define delta ring. @)
df-dring @a |- DRing = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
 { <. 1 , ( l TPEndo p ) >. ,
   <. 2 , ( +g ` ( l ERing p ) ) >. ,
   <. 3 , ( .r ` ( l ERing p ) ) >. } ) @.

@( Define constructed partial vector space A. @)
df-dveca @a |- DVecA = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> ( ( l DRing p )
u. { <. 4 , ( Base ` ( l TGrp p ) ) >. ,
     <. 5 , ( +g ` ( l TGrp p ) ) >. ,
     <. 6 , ( s e. ( l TGrpEndo p ) , f e. ( l Trn p ) |->
            ( s ` f ) ) >. } ) ) @.

@( Define preliminary projective subspace isomorphism. @)
df-dvisopre @a |- DVIsoPre = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
 ( x e. { y e. ( PSubSp ` l ) | y C_ ( l ww p ) } |-> { f e. ( l Trn p ) |
 ( ( l trP p ) ` f ) C_ x } ) ) @.

@( Define constructed partial vector space B. @)
df-dvecb @a |- DVecB = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> ( ( l DRing p )
u. { <. 4 , ( Base ` ( l DRing p ) ) >. ,
     <. 5 , ( +g ` ( l DRing p ) ) >. ,
     <. 6 , ( .r ` ( l DRing p ) ) >. } ) ) @.

@( Define constructed vector space. @)
df-dvechOLD @a |- DVecH = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
    ( ( l DVecA p ) o+ ( l DVecB p ) ) ) @.

@( Define e vector. @)
df-ee @a |- ee = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
  <. ( 0v ` ( l DVecA p ) ) , ( 1r ` ( l DRing p ) ) >. ) @.

@( Define projective subspace isomorphism A. @)
df-dvisoa @a |- DVIsoA = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
 ( x e. { y e. ( PSubSp ` l ) | y C_ ( l ww p ) } |->
  <. ( ( l DVIsoPre p ) ` x ) , ( 0v ` ( l DVecB p ) ) >. ) ) @.

@( Define q-translation. @)
df-qtr @a |- qtr = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
( q e. ( l WAtoms p ) |->
  <. ( iota f ( f e. ( l Trn p ) /\ ( f ` { p } ) = q ) ) ,
      ( 0v ` ( l DVecA p ) ) >. ) ) @.

@( Define projective subspace isomorphism B. @)
df-dvisob @a |- DVIsoB = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
( q e. ( l WAtoms p ) |-> { v e. ( l DVecH p ) | E. s e. ( l DRing p )
   v = ( s ( .s ` ( l DVecH p ) )

( ( l ee p ) ( vadd ( l DVecH p ) ) ( ( l qtr p ) q ) ) ) } ) ) @.

@( Define projective subspace isomorphism C. @)
df-dvisoc @a |- DVIsoC = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
 ( x e. { y e. ( PSubSp ` l ) | -. y C_ ( l ww p ) } |->
    ( iota z A. q e. ( l WAtoms p ) z = ( ( ( l DVIsoB p ) ` q )
          ( +g ` ( l DVecH p ) )
       ( ( l DVIsoA p ) ` ( x i^i ( l ww p ) ) ) ) ) ) ) @.

@( Define projective subspace isomorphism. @)
df-dvisoh @a |- DVIsoH = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
      ( ( l DVIsoA p ) u. ( l DVIsoC p ) ) ) @.

@( Define constructed orthocomplement. @)
df-soc @a |- S_|_ = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
    ( s e. ( SubSpNEW ` ( l DVecH p ) ) |->
      ( ( _|_P ` l ) ` ( `' ( l DVIsoH p ) ` s ) ) ) ) @.

@( Define the opposite of a ring with multiplication reversed. @)
df-ropp @a |- Ropp = ( r e. _V |-> ( ( r |` ( _V \ { 3 } ) ) u.
  { <. 3 , ( x e. ( Base ` r ) , y e. ( Base ` r ) |->
      ( y ( .r ` r ) x ) ) >. } ) ) @.

@( Define the left dual of a vector space. @)
df-vldual @a |- Vldual = ( v e. _V |-> ( ( v |` ( _V \ ( 3 ... 6 ) ) ) u.
  { a | E. l E. k E. t E. u E. w (
      ( k = ( Base ` v )
        /\ t = ( .r ` ( Ropp ` v ) )
        /\ u = ( vbase ` v ) )
    /\ ( w = { g | ( g : u --> k /\ A. r e. k A. x e. u
              ( g ` ( r ( .s ` v ) x ) ) = ( ( g ` x ) t r ) ) }
         /\ a e. ( { <. 3 , t >. , <. 4 , w >. } u.
              { <. 5 , ( g e. v , h e. v |-> ( x e. u |->
                  ( ( g ` x ) ( +g ` v ) ( h ` x ) ) ) ) >. ,
                <. 6 , ( r e. k , g e. v |-> ( x e. u |->
                  ( r t ( g ` x ) ) ) ) >. } ) ) ) } ) ) @.

@( Define vector domain. @)
df-vecdom @a |- vecdom = ( w e. _V |->
         ( iota d A. f e. ( vbase ` w ) d = dom f ) ) @.

@( Define kernel of a functional. @)
df-ker @a |- ker = ( w e. _V |-> ( f e. ( vbase ` w ) |->
   { x e. ( vecdom ` w ) | ( f ` x ) = ( 0g ` w ) } ) ) @.

@( Define one-dimensional subspace map. @)
df-mapd @a |- mapd = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> { a | E. v E. w
 ( v = ( l DVecH p ) /\ w = ( Vldual ` v )
   /\ a e. ( s e. { r | E. x e. ( vbase ` v )
      r = ( ( span ` v ) ` { x } ) } |->
           ( iota t A. x e. s A. f e. ( vbase ` w )

( ( ( ker w ) f ) = s /\ t = ( ( span w ) { f } ) ) ) ) ) } ) @.

@( Define e vector image. @)
df-eimage @a |- eimage = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> { a | E. v E. w E. e
    ( ( v = ( l DVecH p ) /\ w = ( Vldual ` v )
      /\ e = ( l ee p ) )
       /\ a e. ( iota f ( f e. ( ( l mapd p ) ` ( ( spanNEW ` v ) ` { e } )
            ) /\ ( f ` e ) = ( 1r ` w ) ) ) ) } ) @.

@( Define h map. @)
df-hmap @a |- hmap = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> { a | E. v E. w E. e E. f

( ( v = ( l DVecH p ) /\ w = ( Vldual v ) /\ e = ( l ee p ) ) /\ ( f = ( l eimage p ) /\ a e. ( y e. ( vbase v ) |-> if ( y = ( 0v v ) , ( 0v w ) , if ( y e. ( ( spanNEW v ) { e } ) , ( iota u ( u e. ( ( spanNEW w ) { f } ) /\ ( u e ) = ( f y ) ) ) , ( iota u ( u e. ( vbase w ) /\ ( ( l mapd p ) ( ( spanNEW v ) { y } ) ) = ( ( spanNEW w ) { v } ) /\ ( ( l mapd v ) ( ( span v ) { ( e ( -vNEW v ) y ) } ) ) = ( ( span w ) { ( f ( -vNEW ` w ) u ) } ) ) ) ) ) ) ) ) } ) @.

@( Define g map. @)
df-gmap @a |- gmap = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |-> { a | E. v E. w E. e E. f

( v = ( l DVecH p ) /\ w = ( Vldual v ) /\ a e. ( f e. ( vbase v ) |-> ( iota g ( g e. ( Base w ) /\ A. x e. ( vbase v ) ( ( l hmap p ) ( f ( .s v ) x ) ) = ( g ( .s w ) ( ( l hmap l ) x ) ) ) ) ) ) } ) @.

@( Define Hilbert space constructed from Hilbert lattice. @)
df-hltohil @a |- HLtoHil = ( l e. _V , p e. _V |->
   ( ( l DVecH p ) u.
     { <. 7 , ( l gmap p ) >. ,
       <. 8 , ( a e. ( vbase ` ( l DVecH p ) ) , b e.

( vbase ( l DVecH p ) ) |-> ( ( ( l hmap p ) b ) ` a ) ) >. } ) ) @. @}

pmap

Extend class notation with set of all "lattice lines" (lattice elements which cover an atom) in a Hilbert lattice.

Axiom: clln


class LLines

Extend class notation with set of all "lattice planes" (lattice elements which cover a line) in a Hilbert lattice.

Axiom: clpl


class LPlanes

Extend class notation with set of all 3-dimensional "lattice volumes" (lattice elements which cover a plane) in a Hilbert lattice.

Axiom: clvol


class LVols

Extend class notation with set of all projective lines for a Hilbert lattice.

Disjoint


a k p q r s x

Define the set of all "lattice lines" (lattice elements which cover an atom) in a Hilbert lattice k , in other words all elements of height 2 (or lattice dimension 2 or projective dimension 1). (Contributed by NM, 16-Jun-2012.)

Axiom: df-llines


|- LLines = ( k e. _V |-> { x e. ( Base ` k ) | E. p e. ( Atoms ` k ) p ( <o ` k ) x } )

Define the set of all "lattice planes" (lattice elements which cover a line) in a Hilbert lattice k , in other words all elements of height 3 (or lattice dimension 3 or projective dimension 2). (Contributed by NM, 16-Jun-2012.)

Axiom: df-lplanes


|- LPlanes = ( k e. _V |-> { x e. ( Base ` k ) | E. p e. ( LLines ` k ) p ( <o ` k ) x } )

Define the set of all 3-dimensional "lattice volumes" (lattice elements which cover a plane) in a Hilbert lattice k , in other words all elements of height 4 (or lattice dimension 4 or projective dimension 3). (Contributed by NM, 1-Jul-2012.)

Axiom: df-lvols


|- LVols = ( k e. _V |-> { x e. ( Base ` k ) | E. p e. ( LPlanes ` k ) p ( <o ` k ) x } )

Define set of all projective lines for a Hilbert lattice (actually in any set at all, for simplicity). The join of two distinct atoms equals a line. Definition of lines in item 1 of [Holland95] p. 222. (Contributed by NM, 19-Sep-2011.)

Axiom: df-lines


|- Lines = ( k e. _V |-> { s | E. q e. ( Atoms ` k ) E. r e. ( Atoms ` k ) ( q =/= r /\ s = { p e. ( Atoms ` k ) | p ( le ` k ) ( q ( join ` k ) r ) } ) } )

Define set of all projective points in a Hilbert lattice (actually in any set at all, for simplicity). A projective point is the singleton of a lattice atom. Definition 15.1 of [MaedaMaeda] p. 61. Note that item 1 in [Holland95] p. 222 defines a point as the atom itself, but this leads to a complicated subspace ordering that may be either membership or inclusion based on its arguments. (Contributed by NM, 2-Oct-2011.)

Axiom: df-pointsN


|- Points = ( k e. _V |-> { q | E. p e. ( Atoms ` k ) q = { p } } )

Define set of all projective subspaces. Based on definition of subspace in [Holland95] p. 212. (Contributed by NM, 2-Oct-2011.)

Axiom: df-psubsp


|- PSubSp = ( k e. _V |-> { s | ( s C_ ( Atoms ` k ) /\ A. p e. s A. q e. s A. r e. ( Atoms ` k ) ( r ( le ` k ) ( p ( join ` k ) q ) -> r e. s ) ) } )

Define projective map for k at a . Definition in Theorem 15.5 of [MaedaMaeda] p. 62. (Contributed by NM, 2-Oct-2011.)

Axiom: df-pmap


|- pmap = ( k e. _V |-> ( a e. ( Base ` k ) |-> { p e. ( Atoms ` k ) | p ( le ` k ) a } ) )

Essential: dath.e

Essential: dath.f


|- F = ( ( R .\/ P ) ./\ ( U .\/ S ) )

Desargues' Theorem of projective geometry (proved for a Hilbert lattice). Assume each triple of atoms (points) P Q R and S T U forms a triangle (i.e. determines a plane). Assume that lines P S , Q T , and R U meet at a "center of perspectivity" C . (We also assume that C is not on any of the 6 lines forming the two triangles.) Then the atoms D = ( P .\/ Q ) ./\ ( S .\/ T ) , E = ( Q .\/ R ) ./\ ( T .\/ U ) , F = ( R .\/ P ) ./\ ( U .\/ S ) are colinear, forming an "axis of perspectivity".

   Our proof roughly follows Theorem 2.7.1, p. 78 in Beutelspacher and
   Rosenbaum, _Projective Geometry:  From Foundations to Applications_,
   Cambridge University Press (1988).  Unlike them, we don't assume ` C `
   is an atom to make this theorem slightly more general for easier future
   use.  However, we prove that ` C ` must be an atom in ~ dalemcea .

   For a visual demonstration, see the "Desargue's Theorem" applet at
   ~ http://www.dynamicgeometry.com/JavaSketchpad/Gallery.html .  The
   points I, J, and K there define the axis of perspectivity.

   See theorem ~ dalaw for Desargues Law, which eliminates all of the
   preconditions on the atoms except for central perspectivity.  This is
   Metamath 100 proof #87.  (Contributed by NM, 20-Aug-2012.)

C .<_ ( Q .\/ R ) /\ -. C .<_ ( R .\/ P ) ) /\ ( -. C .<_ ( S .\/ T ) /\ -. C .<_ ( T .\/ U ) /\ -. C .<_ ( U .\/ S ) ) /\ ( C .<_ ( P .\/ S ) /\ C .<_ ( Q .\/ T ) /\ C .<_ ( R .\/ U ) ) ) ) -> F .<_ ( D .\/ E ) )
